[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m478[0m[39m:               if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr == end[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m479[0m[39m:               [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m  sprintf [0m[1;39m([0m[39merror, [0m[32m"%d:%d: EOF unexpected"[0m[39m, line_and_col[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m912[0m[39m:   return root;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/json.[0m[1;92mc:955[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m959[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m955[0m[39m:json_value * json_parse [0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst json_char * json, size_t length[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m956[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m957[0m[39m:   json_settings settings = [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m958[0m[39m:   return json_parse_ex [0m[1;39m([0m[39m&settings, json, length, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m959[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis Summary[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the evaluation report and code snippets, I've identified the root [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause of the heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability. The crash occurs at line [0m[1;36m620[0m[39m in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/json.c` during the parsing of the JSON keyword `false`, but this is part of a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msystematic off-by-one error pattern that appears in [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m locations throughout the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`json_parse_ex` function.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability stems from incorrect boundary checks when using pre-increment [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointer operations. The pattern appears as:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < N || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'x'[0m[39m || [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**The Issue:**[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `end - state.ptr` represents bytes from current position [0m[1;39m([0m[39minclusive[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to end [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mexclusive[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Pre-increment `*[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` advances the pointer BEFORE dereferencing[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- With N pre-increments, the code accesses positions: current+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, current+[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m, [0m[33m...[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcurrent+N[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- To safely access current+N, we need: `end - state.ptr > N`[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The check should fail when: `end - state.ptr <= N`, which is equivalent to `end -[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstate.ptr < N+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Current checks are off-by-one:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- They use `< N` when they should use `< N+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This allows reading one byte past the buffer boundary[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Evaluation Report Context[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe crash report shows:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Input: [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m-byte buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlikely [0m[32m"false"[0m[39m or [0m[32m"fals\0"[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Crash at line [0m[1;36m620[0m[39m during the 4th pre-increment when parsing `false`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Address [0m[1;36m0x5020000000b5[0m[39m is exactly at the boundary [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m-byte region[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This confirms the off-by-one error allows reading past the allocated buffer[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Affected Locations[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBased on the vulnerability metadata files and code analysis, there are [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m locations [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith identical off-by-one errors:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m** - Unicode escape `\uXXXX` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m pre-increments[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m** - UTF-[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m surrogate pair [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m6[0m[39m pre-increments[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m602[0m[39m** - Keyword `true` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m3[0m[39m pre-increments[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m618[0m[39m** - Keyword `false` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m pre-increments[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ← **Evaluation Report crash**[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m633[0m[39m** - Keyword `null` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m3[0m[39m pre-increments[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Fix Line [0m[1;36m618[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPrimary Issue from Evaluation Report[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLocate the boundary check for the `false` keyword parsing:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'a'[0m[39m ||[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'l'[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m's'[0m[39m ||[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change:** Modify the check from `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` to `< [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m`[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification:** The code performs [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m pre-increments, requiring access to [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpositions current+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m through current+[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. To safely access current+[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, we need at least[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m bytes remaining [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr >= [0m[1;36m5[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so the check should fail when `end - [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstate.ptr < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m`.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Fix Line [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUnicode Escape Sequence[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLocate the boundary check for Unicode escape sequences:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b1 = hex_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[39m ||[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b2 = hex_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[39m ||[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b3 = hex_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[39m ||[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b4 = hex_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change:** Modify the check from `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` to `< [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m`[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification:** Same reasoning as above - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m pre-increments require [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m bytes.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Fix Line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUTF-[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m Surrogate Pair[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLocate the boundary check for surrogate pair parsing:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'\\' || [0m[32m([0m[32m*++ state.ptr[0m[32m)[0m[32m != '[0m[39mu' ||[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b1 = hex_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[39m ||[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b2 = hex_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[39m ||[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b3 = hex_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[39m ||[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m([0m[39muc_b4 = hex_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change:** Modify the check from `< [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m` to `< [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m`[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification:** [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m pre-increments require [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes remaining.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Fix Line [0m[1;36m602[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mKeyword [0m[32m'true'[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change:** Modify the check from `< [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m` to `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification:** [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m pre-increments require [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes remaining.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m: Fix Line [0m[1;36m633[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mKeyword [0m[32m'null'[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLocate the boundary check for the `null` keyword:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'u'[0m[39m ||[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'l'[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'l'[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change:** Modify the check from `< [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m` to `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification:** [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m pre-increments require [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes remaining.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Rationale[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes:** Only modifies the boundary check constants, changing single[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnumeric literals in [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m locations[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Surgical Precision:** Targets the exact root cause without affecting [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msurrounding logic[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Pattern Consistency:** Applies the same fix pattern to all instances of the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Proven Solution:** The provided patches in the vulnerability metadata [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdemonstrate this exact approach works[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **No Functional Changes:** Only makes boundary checks more restrictive[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Same Error Handling:** Still uses the same error paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39me_unknown_value, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39me_failed[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Two-Pass Architecture Intact:** Doesn't modify the parsing strategy or data [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstructures[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **API Compatibility:** External interfaces remain unchanged[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Existing Valid Inputs:** All valid JSON inputs will still parse correctly[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Only Rejects Invalid Inputs Earlier:** Truncated or malformed inputs that [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwould have caused buffer overflows now fail the boundary check and return an error[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Evaluation Report[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Directly Fixes Crash Location:** Line [0m[1;36m618[0m[39m modification prevents the exact [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrash scenario in the evaluation report[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Comprehensive Solution:** Fixes all [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m instances of the same vulnerability [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern, not just the one that crashed[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Validated Approach:** The good patches in the vulnerability metadata files [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirm this solution[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Memory Safety:** Eliminates all heap buffer over-read vulnerabilities [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mCWE-[0m[1;36m126[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effects:**[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **More Restrictive Validation:** Truncated inputs that previously might have been[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mread [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsafely[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will now be rejected earlier[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Error Messages:** May trigger errors at slightly different locations for [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalformed inputs[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- These are NOT negative side effects - they represent correct behavior[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Invalid/truncated JSON should be rejected, not parsed with buffer overflows[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Error handling already exists and will function correctly[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No impact on valid JSON parsing[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Reference to Similar Patterns in Codebase[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase already demonstrates correct boundary checking in other locations:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m242[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m BOM[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:** Uses `length >= [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m` before accessing [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m bytes ✓[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m462[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mBlock comments[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:** Uses `state.ptr < [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before accessing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`state.ptr[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` ✓[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m478[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mComment parsing[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:** Increments then checks `== end` before [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdereferencing ✓[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThese patterns confirm that proper boundary checking is the established approach in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe codebase. The fixes align with these existing patterns and correct the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minconsistencies.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
